公司简介

 	
PUTRA ABADI TRANS is a full service International Freight Forwarder and Logistics company, has been established since year of 1984 with a vision to become a market leader of this business. Right now, we have become one of the most stable and dedicated company into this business with our comprehensive menu of service and experience for over than 35 years.

PUTRA ABADI TRANS, with ours comprehensive range of services, provides an integrated total logistics service solution by air, ocean, inland transportation and warehousing service to our customer. We employ air, ocean and inland transportation specialists who possess proven analytic and operations expertise. They maintain a dedicated work ethic to do everything possible to satisfy the clients service requirements.

We are a forward thinking logistics provider - always seeking to provide a better service for our valuable customers. Our aim is to create and maintain a reputation as the market leader in customer service, continually seeking new and attractive value propositions for our clients through a world-class business management expertise in our operations.

We have our head office in Jakarta and cover all Indonesian main ports i.e. Jakarta, Surabaya, Semarang, Bali, Medan, Makassar, Balikpapan, Bandung and major cities in this country. 公司简介

Mabua Jafe Raya is a freight forwarding and logistics company based in Jakarta, Indonesia which established in 2019. We have professional team player with decade of experience in the field of freight forwarding. Not only focusing on domestic deliveries, but our company also serves international, export & import deliveries. Mabua Jafe Raya provides a complete range of services such as:

Air Freight, Ocean Freight, Land Transport, Expedited and Consolidated, Warehousing, Dry Cargo (20'FT, 40'FT, 40'HC, and 45'HC), Special Cargo (Open Top, Flat Rack, Tank Tainer / Isotank, and Reefer), Break Bulk, Project Cargo, Dangerous Goods Handling, Pharmaceutical & Perishable Goods, Insurance, and Custom Clearance. Our Ocean service capabilities include Full Container load (FCL) and Less than container load (LCL).

Reliable, responsive and understanding these are the traits that define our company.

We approach every need of our customer with utmost flexibility because we concentrate not on the processes but the end result, proper delivery of the shipment.

Why Mabua Jafe Raya? 

Our experience in handling catalyst deliveries for clients as big as Pertamina an (Indonesian state-owned oil and natural gas corporation based in Jakarta) is proof of our commitment to providing the best service in the logistics industry. 
As well our recent project to successfully shipped 4,000 tons of Used Cooking Oil using Break Bulk vessel from Banten, Indonesia to Louisiana, USA. 
Not to mention we also honoured to deliver safely export project cargo with Helicopter parts as the commodity until destination.

We always prioritize quality, safety and availability at every stage of delivery, making each of our projects a top priority. We are happy to show our achievements in completing the delivery of our customer goods. We have succeeded in providing reliable and efficient logistics services to deliver these products to our customers safely and on time. This success is a reflection of our commitment to providing the best solutions in the world of logistics, as well as our dedication to meeting our clients needs. This success is proof of our commitment to providing the best freight forwarding services, ensuring timely, safe and efficient delivery. This achievement strengthens our position as a reliable and professional logistics partner.

公司简介

Since its foundation in 2003, PT Freight Cargo Logistics(FCL) has
continued to grow for more than 17 years, and it is now regarded as
the one of the top 3 Forwarders in terms of Indonesia’s sea/air export
and import cargo handling volume. (Averagely 1500 conts.). FCL provides the entire range of logistics services to global customers,
making it Indonesia’s best total logistics service provider. FCL does offer the services not only just as a forwarder but also a
consolidator. We specialize in opening console box with aiming to meet the customers various needs perfectly by putting customers demand first and considering things from their point of view.
Starting from opening consolidation service from/to Busan in 2005, It
has expanded the console areas with Shanghai, Hong Kong, Bangkok,
Taiwan and Ho Chi Minh, Hanoi. These routes are all direct regular
console service and open 1 box every week at least. (Some area open
2 boxes per week) and it is still in an effort to expand its area. At PT Freight Cargo Logistics, we do specialize in transporting ocean
and air cargo and offer excellent services with cost competitiveness
and customer oriented mind which are enough to fulfill our role as
best logistics business partner. Please watch how we do to provide
the best service to our customers.

公司简介

COMPANY

CV. UMO INDONESIA. is one of the fully established & leading Customs House Agents / International Freight Forwarding Agents, handling clearance of Import & Export Cargo from Tg. Priok – Jakarta, Tg. Emas – Semarang, Tg. Perak, Surabaya, Belawan – Medan & Airport in Soekarno Hatta. Further, CV. UMO INDONESIA has a team of professionals having experience of more than 9 years from 1997 in the trade and are well versed with Customs Rules & Regulations.

We are committed to Total Quality Management ( TQM) services and our team of employees are not only highly experienced but also individually dedicated to speedy execution of assignments with decentralisation of authority at various levels.

We offer a  service to our customers – ONE POINT INFORMATION a hallmark in the services offered by CV. UMO INDONESIA. With our strong infrastructure facilities and connectivity with major ports in Indonesia, the status of any consignment can be obtained from a “ Single Point” . All our Branches are well connected with modern communication systems.

CV. UMO INDONESIA offers you a ‘ Complete Logistic Solutions’ to enable you to meet the challenges of International Trade. In fact, we go the extra mile to maintain your commitments as your commitments is our Business.

Delivery right on time – every time – is our driving force. We reach… .. where Eagle dares… 
 
 In short, CV. UMO INDONESIA is “ PROFESSIONAL’ S ULTIMATE DESTINATION” .

SERVICES

Our Core Services Include
We are proud ourselves on our Professionalism and Integrity with instant communication with our prestigious clients. We are able to offer following range of services to our various clients with respect to packaging warehousing and transportation facilities through our strong & reliable associates.

Core Services: 
 ? Customs Clearances of Export & Import consignments
? Air & Sea freight for Exports & Imports
? Project Forwarding
? Liaison with Government Agencies

Logistics Services: 
 ? Distribution & Warehousing
? Transportation
? Consultancy Services
? Indenting Services

Customs Clearance
Imports / Exports / Logistics Services

Imports: 
 Prior Documentation: 
 As soon as vance set of documents received, the documentation process starts with respect to classification of items for  possible benefit to the Customer with reference to various Customs Notifications / exemptions etc., are being examined by a team of experts at CV. UMO INDONESIA. The pro-active-anticipation of problems by our experts enable our Customers not only avoid the delay in clearance but also heavy demurrage, detention charges etc., which account of huge financial loss.

Pre-Alert Message: 
 After necessary formalities are completed, the Customer is informed about the “ Customs Duty” and other statutory payments ( if any) . The customers can plan disbursement of goods and logistics, even before the arrival of shipment at Godown / Factory.

Exports: 
 Cargo Pick Up: 
 The freight forwarding cycle begins with cargo pick up from the Vendor’ s factory. The cargo is then transported to warehouse near the port of loading by train or truck, depending on factors like volume of cargo shipping deadlines and other parameters. The local State and Central Octroi / Transportation and other formalities like and others are adequately covered.

Verification/ Measurement of Cargo: 
 When the cargo from vendor’ s factory reaches the warehouse, it is first measured and weighted by authorized surveyors. The size of the container is decided based on the survey report. The customer is then intimated about verification details.

Pre-Alert Message: 
 After necessary formalities are completed at customs & port and the container is loaded on the vessel, we send a message along with the necessary shipping documents.

Clearance Time: 
 We understand the gravity of the “ Transit Time for clearance” and hence we put our best efforts to clear any given shipments at the earliest possi

公司简介

COMPANY

CV. UMO INDONESIA. is one of the fully established & leading Customs House Agents / International Freight Forwarding Agents, handling clearance of Import & Export Cargo from Tg. Priok – Jakarta, Tg. Emas – Semarang, Tg. Perak, Surabaya, Belawan – Medan & Airport in Soekarno Hatta. Further, CV. UMO INDONESIA has a team of professionals having experience of more than 9 years from 1997 in the trade and are well versed with Customs Rules & Regulations.

We are committed to Total Quality Management ( TQM) services and our team of employees are not only highly experienced but also individually dedicated to speedy execution of assignments with decentralisation of authority at various levels.

We offer a  service to our customers – ONE POINT INFORMATION a hallmark in the services offered by CV. UMO INDONESIA. With our strong infrastructure facilities and connectivity with major ports in Indonesia, the status of any consignment can be obtained from a “ Single Point” . All our Branches are well connected with modern communication systems.

CV. UMO INDONESIA offers you a ‘ Complete Logistic Solutions’ to enable you to meet the challenges of International Trade. In fact, we go the extra mile to maintain your commitments as your commitments is our Business.

Delivery right on time – every time – is our driving force. We reach… .. where Eagle dares… 
 
 In short, CV. UMO INDONESIA is “ PROFESSIONAL’ S ULTIMATE DESTINATION” .

SERVICES

Our Core Services Include
We are proud ourselves on our Professionalism and Integrity with instant communication with our prestigious clients. We are able to offer following range of services to our various clients with respect to packaging warehousing and transportation facilities through our strong & reliable associates.

Core Services: 
 ? Customs Clearances of Export & Import consignments
? Air & Sea freight for Exports & Imports
? Project Forwarding
? Liaison with Government Agencies

Logistics Services: 
 ? Distribution & Warehousing
? Transportation
? Consultancy Services
? Indenting Services

Customs Clearance
Imports / Exports / Logistics Services

Imports: 
 Prior Documentation: 
 As soon as vance set of documents received, the documentation process starts with respect to classification of items for  possible benefit to the Customer with reference to various Customs Notifications / exemptions etc., are being examined by a team of experts at CV. UMO INDONESIA. The pro-active-anticipation of problems by our experts enable our Customers not only avoid the delay in clearance but also heavy demurrage, detention charges etc., which account of huge financial loss.

Pre-Alert Message: 
 After necessary formalities are completed, the Customer is informed about the “ Customs Duty” and other statutory payments ( if any) . The customers can plan disbursement of goods and logistics, even before the arrival of shipment at Godown / Factory.

Exports: 
 Cargo Pick Up: 
 The freight forwarding cycle begins with cargo pick up from the Vendor’ s factory. The cargo is then transported to warehouse near the port of loading by train or truck, depending on factors like volume of cargo shipping deadlines and other parameters. The local State and Central Octroi / Transportation and other formalities like and others are adequately covered.

Verification/ Measurement of Cargo: 
 When the cargo from vendor’ s factory reaches the warehouse, it is first measured and weighted by authorized surveyors. The size of the container is decided based on the survey report. The customer is then intimated about verification details.

Pre-Alert Message: 
 After necessary formalities are completed at customs & port and the container is loaded on the vessel, we send a message along with the necessary shipping documents.

Clearance Time: 
 We understand the gravity of the “ Transit Time for clearance” and hence we put our best efforts to clear any given shipments at the earliest possi

PT. DFI Logistics is a verified member of WCA & WWPC. 
Almost the same with other forwarder agents DFI Logistics are specialized in the handling and shipping of goods by air, ocean and land. However, we offer a ONE STOP SOLUTION - customizing freight forwarding and logistic services to accommodate to the  needs of every client. Ever prolific, DFI Logistics is the trusted name in international freight forwarding. 
We, at DFI Logistics, are truly dedicated to the task of providing skilled and meticulous services to ensure the satisfaction of our valued clients. 
By setting a high-level standard for specialized services with the use of sophisticated technology, DFI Logistics has emerged into the ken of the international freight forwarding business in providing world class solutions - both locally and internationally. 


DFI Logistics has the following services:

- Freight Forwarding. Verified member of www.wcaworld.com 
- Door to Door Logistics
- Warehousing
- LCL Consolidation
- Project Management ----Verified member of www.wwpc.eu.com 
- Custom Clearance
- Flexitanks
- Trucking
- Value Added Services

Apart from that, we are also offering incentive to your good company if you have shipment to Indonesia. 
We offer you USD. 35/shipment if you put our company as the delivery agent in your HOUSE B/L. This is as our compliment to your support and this will not take an effect of higher cost at destination as we take it from the unnecessary expenses that most forwarders here do to every import. 
We cannot make our import local costs lower as it has been a standard cost in our country, they only thing to do is to return it back to our agent.
For any further information needed you can visit to our website at www.dfilogistics.com  feel free to write us message and we will be very happy to give our immediate respond.

首页
M+R Forwarding Indonesia
M+R Forwarding Indonesia
基本信息

雅加达, 印度尼西亚

Jl. Raya Pasar Minggu No.5

1 Jan 1952

101-500

www.mrspedag.com
公司简介

In 1952, young Swiss entrepreneurs Mr. Roger Metzger and Mr. Hansruedi Richner, founded a freight forwarding company in Basel. Focussing initially on road transportation from Germany, activities were step by step expanded. By the mid seventies, the company had grown to a size of some 150 employees, with branch offices in Schaffhausen, Zurich and Geneva.

After the passing away of Mr. Roger Metzger in 1975, the company was led henceforth alone by the remaining founder, Mr. Hansruedi Richner. The company moved into a new area in 1979, with the take-over of SPEDAG SPEDITIONS AG, another Basel-based freight forwarding company established in 1928, with branch offices in Rotterdam, Antwerp and South Africa. Following the acquisition, the companies operated under the trade name of M+R SPEDAG GROUP.

The coming years were marked by a rapid expansion. In Switzerland, the company established itself as one of the leading enterprises in the field of transportation and logistics, specializing in particular on European Overland services, Sea- and Airfreights as well as Textile Logistics. In 1985, M+R Spedag expanded to Asia, where over the course of 20 years it grew from a small presence with offices in Hong Kong and Singapore to an Asia-wide network of own offices. 1998 saw the founding of Spedag East Africa, with operating companies in Uganda, Kenya, Tanzania and Rwanda.

After half a century of commitment to the company group, founding member Hansruedi Richner handed over the management of the company to his son, Daniel Richner. After successor arrangements were completed in 2006, Daniel Richner took over all shares of the company as well as the presidency of the group.
联系我们
Nurman
nurman.sutiawan@id.mrspedag.com
M+R Forwarding Indonesia印度尼西亚

www.pressti-cargo.com
公司简介

PRESSTI CARGO
PT. PRESSTI ASIA INDONESIA
INTERNATIONAL FREIGHT FORWARDER

Merupakan perusahaan freight forwarder yang melayani kegiatan impor dan ekspor dengan standar pelayanan terbaik dan harga yang sangat kompetitif.
Staf perusahaan kami merupakan satu tim energik yang berkomitmen untuk bekerja sesuai dengan prosedur mutu yang sangat terjamin untuk memastikan bahwa setiap pelanggan mendapat pelayanan pribadi yang sangat memuaskan.

Pelayanan Pressti Cargo

JASA FREIGHT FORWARDING
PRESSTI CARGO (PT. PRESSTI ASIA INDONESIA) membantu anda dibidang Freight Forwarding yaitu pengurusan semua pengiriman dan penerimaan barang melalui darat, laut dan udara.

JASA PPJK
PRESSTI CARGO (PT. PRESSTI ASIA INDONESIA) membantu anda dalam kegiatan pengurusan pemenuhan kewajiban pabean untuk dan atas kuasa importir atau eksportir.

JASA EKSPOR-IMPOR
PRESSTI CARGO (PT. PRESSTI ASIA INDONESIA) membantu anda memberikan layanan Jasa Ekspor Impor untuk mengurusi barang yang akan anda ekspor maupun impor.

JASA CUSTOM CLEARENCE
PRESSTI CARGO (PT. PRESSTI ASIA INDONESIA) membantu anda dalam pengurusan customs clearance untuk kegiatan export dan import.

JASA IMPORT DOOR TO DOOR

JL Pulau Payung No 1 TG PRIOK

小于10

http://www.multiterminal.co.id
公司简介

PT Multi Terminal Indonesia (MTI) from the legal aspect confirmed by the Notary Herdimansyah Chaidirsyah Bachelor of Law in Jakarta on February 15, 2002 but a new operation operates on April 15, 2002. PT MTI is a subsidiary of PT (Persero) Pelabuhan Indonesia II, which is a spin off from one of the Branch Division, Port of Tanjung Priok Terminal Business Division (dut). The composition of ownership shares of MTI is 99% owned by PT (Persero) Pelabuhan Indonesia II, and 1% owned by the Maritime Employees Cooperative (KOPEGMAR) Tanjung Priok. The history of PT MTI is inseparable from the history of ports in Indonesia, which has undergone several changes (transformation). Transformation of the port company briefly as follows:

1. Period 1984 - 1992 Management of public ports distinguish between public ports and public port cultivated non cultivated. Management of public ports are arranged by Public Companies (PERUM) Port, while the management of public ports that are not cultivated by the Technical Implementation Unit (UPT) under the Directorate General of Sea Transportation as stipulated in Government Regulation number 11 in 1983. Port PERUM divided by region into PERUM Port I sd IV.

2. Period 1992 - 2002 Status PERUM Port II changed into PT (Persero) Pelabuhan Indonesia II in accordance with Government Regulation number 57 dated October 19, 1991, in this period of loading and unloading activities carried out by the Business Division Branch Terminal Port of Tanjung Priok.

3. Period 2002 - until now Terminal Business Division (Dut) separated (Spin Off) from Port of Tanjung Priok branch to PT Multi Terminal Indonesia which was established by Deed of Company Establishment Deed number 15 by Herdimansyah Chaidirsyah Bachelor of Law in Jakarta on February 15, 2002, based on considerations optimize the business potential and strengthen its competitive advantage as service providers.
联系我们
rolys heru
rolys_at@yahoo.com
PT MTI印度尼西亚

公司简介

PT. ARTHA OCEAN LIGHT (AOL) established in 2003, has diversified it’s traditional freight forwarding activities into a fully integrated logistics provider & is equally involved in air and sea freight operations. The company has grown significantly over the years till today as one of the well trusted logistics provider in Indonesia.

The foundation of our continued success and development is attributed to the competitive advantages that we possess, a strong team of motivated operators with a wealth of experience and professional knowledge and an extensive global network of carefully selected overseas partners.

Our long term aim is based upon the development and maintenance of personal relationships, combined with quality and diverse logistical solutions. 

We are committed to delivering client satisfaction through the excellence of our work and see ourselves as an extension of our client business.


MISSION

To provide complete logistics solutions that are not only efficient but also reliable and affordable

To gain confidence and trust of our valued clients by conducting business with complete honesty and integrity

SERVICES

AOL offers a premium performance guaranteed air and sea freight service delivering with confidence, a cost effective and timed product tailored to your individual requirements.

- Door to door services
- Air Freight 
- Sea Freight (LCL | FCL)
- Export and Import Documentation
- Custom Clearances
- Warehouse and Distribution


AIR FREIGHT

As with other transport modes, we operate state of the art systems that put the benefits of today's technology at the customers disposal. We recognize that customers choose air freight for speed and urgency, and provide a fast efficient back-up that reflects this need

SEA FREIGHT

Ocean transportation is a substantial component of the international supply chain. In today's continually changing market you need the strength of a sound, dynamic and reliable freight forwarder to take care of your ocean freight arrangements. AOL has a solid relationship with all the major shipping lines offering unrivalled standards for global ocean freight. Our market leading partners can provide customized logistic schedules world-wide. 

Our experienced staff takes full responsibility for the complete co-ordination of your shipments from point of origin to final destination. Through our association with all major shipping lines and professional carriers, we deliver your goods efficiently, safely, and most importantly, on time. We ensure better coverage, more sailings and more flexible closing times combined with exceptional rates.

CUSTOMS CLEARANCE 

We offer full services for both imports and exports, covering land and sea. We have global expertise in both commodity classifications and all the various government rules and regulations to ensure rapid clearance of your goods through customs, correct classification of import and export materials whilst continually ensuring that the correct customs duties are paid. 

Our role is to ensure that all import and export cargo moves smoothly without unnecessary delays, whilst complying with all relevant statutory regulations.

Our customs clearance agents are experts in local specifications, classifications and regulations. This on-the-ground knowledge allows them to handle ministration tasks for you swiftly and without complication. 

Our comprehensive range of services includes the preparation of all necessary declarations and reporting to the appropriate authorities. Furthermore it includes electronic pre-filing, customs consultancy and documentation processing as well as security sealing and certification.

Bumi Laut Group is a well-established and growing business group, primarily involved in shipping and logistics oriented businesses, among others:
? Ship owning & Operating;
? Shipping Agencies;
? Ship management (Marine & Technical Services);
? Chartering & Tramping Operations;
? Freight Forwarding & Transportation;
? Project Cargo & Energy Carrier;
? Ship broking.

Bumi Laut Group, which traces its origins to 1892, but at 1922 in Indonesia, at the Port of Belawan Deli, North Sumatra, today consists of several independent operating companies focusing on respective areas of the above mentioned business activities and is Headquartered in Jakarta, the capital city of Indonesia with an extensive network of branch offices all over Indonesia as well as other parts of Asia. It has business associations and strategic alliances worldwide.

Bumi Laut Group employs around 3000 experienced and competent personnel to support and efficiently carry out its business operations.

The Group maintains good contacts with the business communities, private and public sector organizations as well as the Government.

Over the years, Bumi Laut Group has gained knowledge of the industry and the market as well as secured more businesses directly or jointly with its business partners/strategic alliances.


Bumi Laut Group is managed by competent Executives and supervised by eminent Senior Members of the Board. The Group, over the years, has been continuously developing its businesses, its resources and management systems aiming at efficient business operations and a rewarding growth. 公司简介

PT. Cipta Global Servisindo adalah Perusahaan yang bergerak di bidang jasa International Freight Forwarders Customs Clearance Export & Import And Door To Door dan Domestics services, dengan kompetensi yang tinggi hampir di semua aspek pelayanan kargo, serta didukung jaringan yang kuat dan terpercaya untuk bisa menjamin pengiriman barang sampai tujuan.
PT. Cpta Global Servisindo memiliki kemampuan yang sangat baik dalam menangani setiap aspek kebutuhan pengiriman barang-barang anda. kami berkomitmen untuk menjadi mitra bisnis yang bisa diandalkan dan terpercaya dalam hal jasa pengiriman Export - impor & door to door dan Domestics
Menyadari pentingnya aset yang menunjang dalam mendukung operasional perusahaan, PT. Cipta Global Servisindo memiliki gudang di China terletak di Guangzhou, Yiwu dan mempunyai mitra-mitra di negara lainnya.
Jenis barang yang sudah biasa kami tangani antara lain: Plastik (bijih, kertas PVC, kaca film, fancy, stationery, drilling, genset/spare parts, mesin cetak, mesin bekas, aksesoris, spare parts motor,  mobil, tools, furniture, elekticals equipment, gps, chemicals, mesin bubut, dan masih banyak jenis lainnya yang tidak kami uraikan.
Untuk ekspor sendiri kami memiliki agents yang di berbagai Negara dengan rate yang kompetitif. Saat ini kami kuat untuk pengiriman ke wilayah Asia seperti Singapura, Thailand, Filipina, India dan China, Hong Kong, Malaysia, sedangkan untuk wilayah di luar Asia seperti Amerika Serikat, Afrika Selatan (Cape Town dan Durban), Italy. Untuk planning shipment full container yang rutin per bulan, kami akan berikan rate spesial.
Sampai saat ini para customer kami masih setia menggunakan jasa kami, karena kepercayaan dari mereka selalu mampu kami jaga mulai dari pengiriman dan pengurusan sampai ke tempat tujuan. 
Untuk perusahaan yang belum memiliki pensyaratan import, kami menyediakan fasilitas kelengkapan pabean / UNDER NAME
Besar harapan kami dapat menjadi mitra dengan perusahaan anda.

PT FPS INDONESIA

All sources are addressed to generate such output with focus on satisfaction of the customers which is mostly identified as a  ones. For this purpose, consistently should be a prerequisite for all of processes of service delivery by which long term relationship can be created and maintaining for mutual benefit can be achieved. To constitute this purpose, the management has been and continually committed to establish, implement, maintain and improve the subscribed management systems.

It is Mr. Iskandar Zulkarnain, the founder of ISKA NIAGA DARMA GROUP and Famous Pacific Shipping Group of Network Companies who involve to lead the company at time being since the beginning (1991) and after its autonomous (2006) with the focus on LCL Consolidation, complement with related services such as NVOCC, domestic transporter, customs clearance broker, packing provider, project cargo handling and all related services in managing moving of cargoes. Supported by 13 branch offices spread out from Medan (North Sumatera) at the west to Mataram (East Nusa Tenggara) at the east, FPS Indonesia keep on track to go faster and faster to face inevitability of globalization.

Since establishing, FPS Indonesia altogether with overseas network agents has introduced the brand of "FPS - Famous Pacific Shipping" in a carefully managed fashion. Rolling-out the brand extensively to key regional markets in Asia, thus promoting Indonesia as an  opportunity to enhance its credibility and standing; and therefore, allow it to strengthen the brand internationally.

公司简介

Dear Sir,

We are looking for china agent to handle our Airfright & Seafreight Cargo.

There are few types of jobs that we need, as follows:

You will be our representative office in China, and you will arrange to pick up the goods from many shipper. It could be the shipper will send the goods to your warehouse, or you'll pick up the goods.

After that, there are three possibilities:

1. If the goods have been sufficient for the fit in one container, it will fit into the container FCL to Jakarta or other destination port.

2. Directly sent to Jakarta by LCL or Airfreight.

3. Sent to several agents in baiyun district or in other areas in china.


Therefore, please send it costs for the logistics services, so that we can immediately calculate and decide which one best agent we will choose.

Please send it to my address ceo@indoexpress.co.id


Thnks & Best Regards,
Bastian P.S

公司简介

PT. INFINITY INDONESIA dengan nama lain I2-Logistics berkedudukan di Jakarta Timur, kami adalah salah satu perusahaan penyedia LAYANAN JASA TERPADU &  INTERNATIONAL FREIGHT FORWARDING dengan jaringan koneksi pasar internasional telah dikembangkan selama bertahun-tahun menjadi bagian kelompok bisnis dimana tempat beroperasi perdagangan antar negara, kami juga memiliki Legalitas dibidang Import & Export, Sub bidang Trading Agent, Customs Clearance, Logistics dan Distribution.

PT. INFINITY INDONESIA didirikan oleh tim profesional dengan pengetahuan yang mendalam dan pengalaman di bidang pelayanan jasa terpadu, selama bertahun-tahun telah menangani berbagai jenis komoditas pengiriman kargo baik import maupun export dari berbagai negara asal.

PT. INFINITY INDONESIA menfokuskan diri pada layanan Jasa Terpadu yang mampu menangani setiap pengiriman baik via Laut atau udara, termasuk dengan penanganan Customs Clearance di wilayah Pabean setempat sampai barang dikirim ke gudang importir, dengan sistem pelayanan handal, cepat, tanggap kepada satu titik informasi oleh dukungan fasilitas teknologi sehingga kami selalu terdepan dalam memberikan informasi kepada semua costumers & relasi bisnis.
Kami menawarkan pengiriman internasional, pergudangan, jasa clearance, berbagai dokumentasi impor dan ekspor dan jasa transportasi domestik.

Kenalkan kami lebih dekat karena kami mampu menciptakan dan membangun bisnis anda semakin berkembang dalam persaingan global didunia perdagangan internasional.

Besar harapan kami jika disediakan waktu dan kesempatan untuk bertemu secara langsung dan semoga jadi langkah awal dari terciptanya suatu hubungan kerjasama yang baik dan saling menguntungkan.  

Silahkan contact kami untuk informasi lebih lanjut:

公司简介

PT. Inter Link Indonesia was founded in 2017 in recognition of the increasingly sophisticated needs of international trade.  Inter Link has grown & matured with the ever-expanding international trade community. We have since managed to establish our own offices in Jakarta to serve our clients all across Indonesia & also overseas. Supported through a strong network of overseas agents who are highly trained professionals with integrated information systems, we are dedicated to provide our clients with reliable, efficient and customer driven logistics services.

We serve a key role in the transportation industry by helping companies manage their supply chain and arranging the transportation of their cargo from point A to point B. Our job is to make our clients' jobs easier by taking out the challenges of logistics management from their hands freeing up our clients' time to focus on their core businesses. 

Through our extensive network and expertise in the transportation industry, we show our clients the best method and help them get the best price for their logistics solutions, allowing our clients to concentrate on the core focus of their businesses.

公司简介

PT. KANA CARGO adalah perusahaan spesialist dalam pengiriman barang ekspor dan impor dengan layanan ‘Door to Door Service’ Melalui layanan ini Kami akan mengangkut barang mulai dari pintu sipengirim sampai ke pintu sipenerima barang. Anda dapat memanfaatkan layanan kami dengan harga terjangkau karena kami menawarkan harga yang kompetitif serta dikombinasikan dengan layanan transportasi cepat ke dan dari berbagai negara di dunia.

“Menangani berbabagai jenis komoditi Import” 
IMPORT DOOR TO DOOR SERVICES Kami menangani pengiriman Import Door to Door anda mulai dari negara asal sampai negara tujuan dan delivery sampai ke Pintu Penerima. Ini yang di namakan Import Door to Door Services.

Kami memberikan kemudahan kepada Pelanggan dengan layanan Door to Door Services. Jasa Kiriman Import Door to Door, Cargo Import Borongan, Import Undername, Import Non Document kami meliputi seluruh komoditas import, dengan harga bersaing dan ketepatan waktu pengiriman membuat kami lebih unggul dari provider lainnya.

PT LV Logistics Indonesia is a freight forwarding company affiliated to LV Shipping & Transport, which was founded in 1921 and has its headquarters is in Vlaardingen, the Netherlands. In Indonesia, we were established in 2012 and in relatively short time has expanded and now has  head office in Jakarta as well as branch offices in Surabaya, Balikpapan, Banjarmasin, and Makassar.

Besides of our global networks of LV Shipping & Transport offices that spread in major cities of five continents, in Indonesia we are also fully backed by skillful and experienced personnel, a full-ranged equipment, and consistently executed operational and safety standards. The combination of those has win the trust of many clients; government companies, private national companies, as well as multinational companies to let PT LV Logistics Indonesia to handle their logistics needs.
 
Our fields of services include   :  

1.      International sea and air freight
2.      Domestic land transport
3.      Integrated warehousing
4.      Domestic and international ship agency
5.      Stevedoring
6.      Chartering of domestic and international cargo
  aircraft and vessel

8.      Import and export customs clearance

公司简介

Dear Sir/Maddam,

We are Pt. Marga  Karya Lestari Indonesia known as Makindo Logistics is an International Freight Forwarder with energetic, capable and experience in shipping, forwarding and consolidation industry and who is still rendering best service with high reputation. In Expanding our business, we would like to build  a mutual cooperation with your esteem company for handling our shipment from your side to Indonesia v.v.

In the meantime please allow us to inform our major standard terms condition of cooperation with our overseas partners for your kind consideration : 

1.	50/50 profit share on ocean/air freight for joint sales, nomination cargo.
2.	supplied rate, ex-work and door charges must be at net-net cost.
3.	Monthly settlement on accounting matter, unless for the total monthly statement of account less than USD 500.00 (United State/Five Hundred) in order to avoid bank charges in both side. It can be considered to the next month account balance, but it would kept as long as 60 days and the payment must made by T/T draft.
4.	We provide our overseas partners a rebate USD 30.00/document for your  shipment going to Jakarta consigned to our company for both LCL and FCL shipment. 
5.	We also provide a rebate for consolidation shipment as below detail : 
Option A 
Rebate 	: USD 155.00/cbm without B/L condition 
Local Charges : USD 90/set + USD 20/cbm (min 2)
W/h charges 	: USD 120/cbm (min 2)
Storage 	: USD 0.40/cbm/days (in case of consignee does not release the   cargo)
Option B 
Rebate 	: USD 170.00/cbm without B/L condition 
Local Charges : USD 90/set + USD 20/cbm (min 2)
W/h charges 	: USD 135/cbm (min 2)
Storage	: USD 0.40/cbm/days (in case of consignee does not release the cargo)

Please kindly study and confirm your acceptance by return message. Many thanks for your kind cooperation. We are looking forward to having a good news from your soon.

Sincerely Yours
Ely Retno
Pt. Makindo Logistics

It had of course, a philosophy meaning. Pigeon often believed as a trustworthy bird for sending message or letter on time, for one place to another. 

The globe means universe, which reflected our access of area in delivering document and package in Indonesia area and worldwide. Due to the early age, we raise spirit & commitment to make great efforts to improve quality of service and build satisfaction to all the customers. Since we have good infrastructure and network support combined with service quality and high integrity of all the employees to fulfill customer’s need, we were not only sell and provide document & package shipment service but also offer practical solution to business industries in developing their service to the for distribution and transportation.

PT. Merpati Alam Semesta (MAS KARGO) with the growth, we develop its service and starting to handling specializing to cater the need for Domestic Express, Freight Forwarding, Warehousing/Distribution, Project Cargo Transportations and Total Logistics.

Since that the time, PT. Merpati Alam Semesta (MAS KARGO) is being develop itself into Integrated Logistics Solution to go towards  reputable National and International company. 公司简介

Dear Sir or Madam,
I would like to Introducing our Company, PT.MUARA ADHI PRAWIRA or better known as MAPMOVING – an easy to remember name which means “the world in my hand”!  We are a premium integrated mover & freight forwarding services company.

We are a young, energetic, highly reputable organization backed up by more than 250 overseas agents across the World. Their agents give us, and ultimately our clients, the support and guarantees to ensure many kind of shipment via air & ocean freight LCL (Less Container Load), FCL (Full Container Load), Break bulking cargo, etc.

MAPMOVING provide  mover & freight forwarding service in Jakarta, Indonesia and our impressive multinational client list is evidence of this. We handle shipments through the main ports of Tanjung Priok or Cengkareng Jakarta, Indonesia and thereafter our shipments are placed in the care of our vetted, reputable worldwide agent-network across the globe.

Our mission is to become an indispensable shipping organization within the highly competitive worldwide market. Our highly trained and experienced personnel, combined with our strong partnerships makes gives us the confidence to achieve this and take on any assignment, large or small.

At our headquarters in Jakarta we have a dedicated workforce of 69 highly trained professionals including the 12 hard working members of our Sales & Marketing department – our staff have many combined years of experience in air & ocean mover & freight forwarding inclusive domestic and inter-Island relocation services and are dedicated to providing  possible service to our clients.  We have operated in the tight, highly competitive Jakarta market and we stand head and shoulders above the competition due to our wealth of experience and our strong customer care focus.  This is continually demonstrated to us in the amount of repeat business we receive from satisfied customers. We consider ourselves as a close family with everyone working for the same goal – complete customer satisfaction!

Yours faithfully,
RM. Yoyo NS Wijoyo
Managing Director

Komp. Bukit Gading Indah Blok Q No. 31

1 Jan 2001

公司简介

Overview
Prolink Multimoda Trans (Sh|tened as PROLINK here below) is an International Freight Forwarder & logistics company. Our headquarter was based in Jakarta, capital of Indonesia, we have branch in Surabaya and representative sub agent at Belawan, Semarang, Bali and Makassar.

Our Service :
International Freight Forwarding : Import & Export by air and sea, General Cargo, Dangerous Cargo and Special Containers.
Inland Transportation : Door to Door Service, Trucking (Container / LCL), Courier by air and Train logistics.
Logistics : Custom Brokerage / License Custom Clearance, Customs Document preparing, Goods Storage / Warehousing, Consolidation, Distribution, Supply Chain, Certificates Issuing (Certificate of Origin), Insurance agents.

Our staff is well-trained, experienced and customer focused. Our marketing team is trade oriented and well versed with requirement of today's global transportation requirements for both imports and exports. With mission of providing logistics solution with high efficiency, we are always ready to serve you for any shipments from / to Indonesia.

Our Vision :
“To be an internationally recognized Logistics Freight Forwarding of excellence, providing comprehensive rates, and service.”

Our Mission :
“We are committed to providing  an optimal service through our dedicated professional workforce.”

Our Value :
“To meet our client’s and partner’s needs and expectations, responsibility, and with efficiently but foremost.”

Freight Forwarding
With personalized services, PROLINK can handle your shipment – regardless of size, point of origin or destination. Through its comprehensive logistics services division, PROLINK can offer you the following services, which you may elect to use individually or as a package:
?	Shipment Booking
?	Bill of Lading Preparation
?	Preparation and Electronic Data Interchange with Custom and Excise
?	Preparation, Consolidation and Forwarding of Export Documents
?	Shipment Monitoring and Project Management

Import Services and Customs Brokerage
PROLINK can offer customized import logistics solutions  to meet your global transportation and customs brokerage requirements. Our import services team is comprised of qualified consultants who will evaluate your entire import process, from collection at the manufacturing facility to delivery at the final destination, and who can process your entries in a timely manner at a competitive cost. Our customers have come to rely on and trust PROLINK and successful history of Customs brokerage services.

Designed to meet your individual requirements, our complete clearance and brokerage services include:
?	Formal and informal entries
?	Warehouse entries
?	Temporary Import Bond (T.I.B.)
?	CFS, Customs bonded warehouses, and indoor and outside yard facilities
?	Duty drawback procedures
?	Tariff classification
?	Electronic entry filing/automated broker interface
?	Other government agencies

Customs Brokerage
PROLINK are committed to developing an import program tailored to further simplify and meet your logistics operation requirements. PROLINK can prepare and submit any and all customs documentation, and help ensure that your shipments are not delayed by customs issues at seaports, airports and at border crossings. With the ever-changing Customs regulatory enhancements, stay updated with  duty saving programs as well as security requirements vital to your supply chain management.
联系我们
Johnny Abbas
info@prolinkmultimoda.com
PT. Prolink Multimoda Trans印度尼西亚

公司简介

PT RICAKUSUMA LESTARI ABADI, well known as RICA, was established in 1994, and in its existence the company has grown in its expertise in logistic arrangement for its customers.   RICA has expertise and plenty of experience in Inbound shipment arrangement and custom clearance, with own team in Jakarta, Semarang and Surabaya. 

RICAis a member of Alpha Pacific Transportation Group(www.alphapacificgroup.com), which started its operation in 1982.  As an Indonesian based group of companies with core business in logistics, the group is equipped with wide ranging specialized expertise from freight forwarders, custom-brokers, warehousing, local & international courier and trucking services.

OUR COMMITMENT
When you trust RICA to handle your shipment, you choose a logistic provider armed with a one stop solution for majority of your needs to and from Indonesia. You will also be working with a partner who understand the global service standard, yet able to adapt them to the challenging local Indonesian environment. 

Our core services include, but not limited to:
* FCL and LCL services
* Regular air export and import volume
* Competitive couriers and small parcel solutions
* Ocean Shipments, International/Domestic routes Private Charter
* Consolidation/De-consolidation/Warehousing
* Cargo Insurance
* Import/Export licensing arrangement in China and Indonesia
* Trade Facilitation
* Delivery Duty Paid shipment (DDP) arrangement to Indonesia
* Trans-loading and/or direct store delivery
* Distribution services within major cities of Indonesia and payment collection
* Own in-house customs clearance team in Jakarta, Semarang and Surabaya
* Own airport office with ability to perform rush handling clearance within 12 hours after shipment arrival

If One-Stop service is a factor that you consider important, RICA is well positioned to serve you.

Although our company is new, but the all the board members and also the staffs came with experiences and background of shipping and forwarding business for more than 20 years.

PT.Sintai Industri Shipyard (SIS)

The company PT. Sintai Industri Shipyard, specialist in the design and build construction of new Ship Building, Fabrication yard, offshore oil and gas facility platform and other drilling equipment fabrication. The business has been successful since year 1995 until now. Based Office on Batam, Indonesia.

Our facilities PT. Sintai Industry Shipyard are covering total area of 7,72 Hectare and Work Shop size: High 12 Meter x Breath 24 Meter x Length 60 Meter. Wharf Size:

Breath 16 Meter x Length 18 Meter (water tide: Low tide 3-4 meter).

Our Fabrication range is listed below for your review:

   1. Ship Builder & Ship Repair
   2. Afloat Ship Repair
   3. Steel Structures
   4. Steel Pipe Works
   5. Weld on connectors (Pin & Box)
   6. Machineries
   7. Electrical
   8. Carpenter & Interior

Our global experience in Ship Builder, Ship Repair (Weld on connectors pipe, fabrication sub sea wellhead on and offshore oil and gas under supervision by drill quip Asia Pasific Pte,Ltd).

PT. Sintai Industri Shipyard and key personnel are qualified with all certificate licenses of Petroleum Industries Associations and management such as safety standards, environment controls, Industry Codes, and Manufacturing Quality Control.

公司简介

PT. DELTA SURYA TEXTILE is a private shareholder company, established  on Tuesday ,24 July 2001, it is targeted to produce good quality spinning yarn for national and international yarn markets.

it is established with 39.340 ring spindles production capacity.

It has continuously progressed in productivity and yarn quality and achieved about 635 tons of spun yarn production per month. The yarn is well accepted in domestic as well export yarn markets and the yearly sales turn over is around 9 million US dollars.

The company has around 600 employees and operates round the clock. It is situated in East Java near Surabaya city.

The company produces  Poly and blended Poly Viscose yarn, range on 12's - 30's for single and 20/2 - 30/2 for double. These yarns are used for knitting as well air jet weaving and the fabrics are being exported.

The company has modern spinning technology with the world class machinery as shown in following page.

PT.JATIDIRI LOGISTIK
PT.JATIDIRI LOGISTIK
基本信息

雅加达, 印度尼西亚

Perkantoran Cempaka Baru Jl. Letjen. Suprapto No.160 Blok B7 Jakarta Pusat 10640 - Indonesia

1 Jan 1989

11-50

www.jatidiritrans.co.id
公司简介

PT. JATIDIRI Logistik was set up in 25th January 1989 by some key personnels who have got vast knowledge & expertise in shipping and freight forwarding industry. It obtained its license in freight forwarding on 3rd May 198. No. AL.003/14/8/W.DKI.JKT-89.

Originally we started our business in export consolidation from Jakarta to Asia, Europe and North America. Then, we began to handle import cargoes (FCL and LCL) from USA, Europe and Asia to Jakarta.

In 1998 with sufficient support from importers/buyers in Jakarta we initiated to do import consolidation from Taiwan and Hongkong to Jakarta. In line with growing demand of importers/buyer in Jakarta for more port coverage, we have expanded our import consolidation from Busan, Shanghai, Osaka, Tokyo, Kobe, Yokohama, Singapore, Bangkok, New Delhi, Mumbai, Ho Chi Minh and Manila to Jakarta, Semarang and Surabaya.

We have been in this freight forwarding business for more than 20 years. Through our long experiences we have acquired the mastery of operational excellence. Equipped with this operational excellence as our competitive edge we can deliver high value of freight forwarding service to our customers.

We fully realize that we exist to serve our customers who will keep supporting us if we can deliver our service to them satisfactorily. We really regard and treat our customers as Kings.
联系我们
Fitria Harini
fitria@jatidiritrans.com
PT.JATIDIRI LOGISTIK印度尼西亚

1 Jan 2003

11-50

公司简介

PT.Lautan Banda Services offer a comprehensive range of Air /Sea Export and Import services. Our global network enables us to provide a complete worldwide transport and logistics solution, no matter what the size, weight, origin or destination.

Our experienced team will advise  cost effective method of moving your freight based on your requirements.

    Airport to Airport
    Airport to Door
    Door to Door
    Consolidations
    Direct and Deferred service
    Export Documentation
    Export Packing and Labeling
    Hanging Garments
    Origin Handing/Inland Transport
    Project Cargo
    Insurance

Services offer a comprehensive range of Sea Export and Import services. Our Global network enables us to provide complete worldwide transport and logistics solutions, no matter what the size, weight, origin or destination.

Sea Freight is generally shipped in 20ft, 40ft and 40ft HC (High Cube) general purposes containers. There is also more specialised equipment available such as 20ft & 40ft Open Top containers, 20ft & 40ft Flat Rack, 20ft & 40ft Platform and 20ft & 40ft Reefer container. These are considered to be specialised equipment therefore the rates are generally more expensive than general purposes containers and the equipment is subject to availability.

Roll On / Roll Off shipping is ideal for cargo such as boats, caravans, motorhomes, trailers and vehicles which are generally driven or wheeled on and off vessels. General/Project cargo can also be shipped as RO/RO, which is known as static cargo.

Lift On / Lift Off shipping is idea for large power boats and sail yachts.

LLS offer customers various shipping options such as:

    Per cbm (LCL – Less than Container Load or Ro/Ro)
    20ft, 40ft and 40ft HC general purpose
    Specialised equipment

Our experienced team will advise  cost effective method of moving your freight based on your requirements.
联系我们
sales
sales@lautanbanda.com
PT.Lautan Banda印度尼西亚

Westline Internasional

Jl. Cipaku 1, Kebayoran Baru, Jakarta Selatan

www.westlinecoal.com
公司简介

Westline started off with product/commodity trading such as iron ore, steam coal, briquette charcoal, and other commodities.  As we progress and built our network of miners, funders & manufacturers we had focus our business mainly in Indonesian origin paper and steam coal.  

We are now well connected to steam coal producers and paper manufacturers in Indonesia. To date we have formed alliances, collaboration and partnership with many companies to strengthen our market presence in both coal and paper business.

For Indonesian origin steam coal, Westline provides a one stop solution for our International clients who are sourcing for Indonesian origin coal.  Westline provide “Local knowledge and International Expertise” that our International clients and partners required.  We cover all grade of coal from low to high calories coal from Indonesia on FOB, CFR and CIF term.  For CFR & CIF term we collaborate with International fund providers who would jointly sign the contract with us and supply to the end buyer/user.

For FOB terms we act as consultant for our International clients where we negotiate contract terms with local suppliers, identify the right source of coal, organize the funding, co-ordinate the shipment, inspect the cargo to ensure cargo readiness before vessel laycan and ensure seller do not failed the International clients which is common sentiment for Indonesian origin coal.

We have our own Indonesian Coal Information Management Plan (ICIMP) that any individual/company can subscribe to receive our weekly published Indonesian origin coal matrix reflecting price trend on FOB & CFR from Small & Medium Enterprises (SME) consolidated from miners & trading houses in Indonesia.  By becoming our subscribers  client would receive many other information and resources other the price with regards to Indonesian origin coal.

Westline is now proud to have very wide network of International clients and local suppliers which we partner and collaborate with in coal & paper business.  Through   our   business   network   and   long   standing   relationship   we were often given privileges, best deals and offered competitive price.  Besides acting as coal consultant we also conduct due diligence on local and foreign companies on behalf of our counter parts.
联系我们
Moh Somir
westline.sg@gmail.com
Westline Internasional印度尼西亚
